Let it crack.\n\n* * *\n\n### ğŸ” **One Bar Only**\n\n*   **Core technique**: Entire song composed from a **single 1-bar loop** â€” _same chord, same groove_ â€” never changes.\n*   **Variation comes from**: FX automation, layering, filtering, muting, volume swells.\n*   **Emotional play**: Forces hypnotic trance or psychotic tension. Either way, youâ€™re _stuck in the loop_.\n\n* * *\n\n### ğŸ§Š **Freeze Pop**\n\n*   **Core technique**: Every sound frozen via granular â€œfreezeâ€ or FFT buffer plugins (e.g. PaulStretch, Spectral Freeze).\n*   **Workflow**: Perform stutters, warps, or pitch bends _inside_ the frozen audio grain field.\n*   **Key plugins**: GRM Tools Freeze, PaulXStretch, Melda Spectral Plugins\n*   **Result**: Popsicles of sound. Hyperarticulated ambient plastic.\n\n* * *\n\n### âš¡ **Ziptone**\n\n*   **Core technique**: **Hard, instantaneous cuts** in pitch, panning, and EQ. No ramps. No automation curves. _Click that switch._\n*   **Inspiration**: Tape stop stabs, modular gate clicks, old-school hard panning.\n*   **Style guide**: Keep everything ultra-clean sonically â€” itâ€™s the cuts themselves that shred.\n\n* * *\n\n### ğŸŒŠ **Washpunk**\n\n*   **Core technique**: **Drums and guitars totally drowned in feedbacking reverb**, mix bus soaked like a wet dog.\n*   **Contrast trick**: Dry vocals or bassline cut through the slop.\n*   **Vibe**: Like the Smashing Pumpkins broke into a church and recorded underwater.\n\n* * *\n\n### ğŸª **Reflexive House**\n\n*   **Core technique**: Every musical part includes _a filtered or delayed version of itself baked in._\n*   **Means**: Bounce the stem, reimport, run through reverb or delay, sidechain it _to its own dry version_.\n*   **Result**: Self-haunted mixdowns. Like each track is remembering what it just did.\n\n* * *\n\n### ğŸ«€ **Compressor Worship**\n\n*   **Core technique**: Every single element in the mix is _aggressively bus-compressed_, even the FX returns.\n*   **Bonus: Feedback Compression** â€” feed the mix bus into a sidechain trigger.\n*   **Sound**: Breathing, surging, _suffocating_. Like techno in a bear hug.\n\n* * *\n\n### ğŸ“ **Quantizecore**\n\n*   **Core technique**: Quantize _everything_. Even ambient textures. Even automation curves.
